","Recommended for the crop requires 4-6 irrigations depending on the soil type and rainfall.Wheat crop requires minimum of 5 irrigations at the following critical stages.
1.Immediately after sowing
2.Crown root initiation: 15-20 DAS 
3.Active tillering stage: 35-40 DAS
4.Flowering stage: 50-55 DAS
5.Grain filling stage: 70-75 DAS

IV- Flowering stage: 50-55 DAS
V- Grain filling stage: 70-75 DAS

"NA","AGRICULTURE","Cereals","Wheat","	Water Management	","Farmer wants to know information about water management in wheat?","Recommended for The crop requires 4 - 6 irrigations depending on the soil type and rainfall. Wheat crop requires minimum of 5 irrigations at the following critical stages.
I – Immediately after sowing
II – Crown root initiation: 15-20 DAS
III- Active tillering stage: 35-40 DAS
IV- Gabot stage: 50-55 DAS
 V- Flowering stage: 70-75 DAS
 VI- Milking stage: 80-85 DAS

 VII- Grain filling stage: 100-105 DAS

Crown root initiation and flowering are the most critical stages. Water stagnation should be voided at the time of germination.
","MADHYA PRADESH","HOSHANGABAD","SEONI MALWA","2019-01-15T15:40:27.217"

"NA","AGRICULTURE","Others","Others","	Field Preparation	","Farmer needs information regarding mushroom production?
","It must first choose which room to be dark, and be neat.
 before 2 days   fumigate room  with formeldyhehyde.
Take wheat, soybean straw or rice straw {not older than 1 year], 
Soak it overnight in 50 liters of water + 3 grams bavistin +75 formalin   solution  then decant it before 2 hours of spanning.
Seprate the seed by crushing them. And fill uppermost and lowermost layer completely with span but in middile laye surface only pot in pripheral region followed by 2-2 inch straw layer . Make 2-3 holes in lower side and 10-15 holes in whole bag, and put it in a slanting surface to get out of remaining water .
After 15-20 days when whitish covering occurs hen hang it on bamboos and irrigate them every evening . Do not get them dried .
Check it out daily when mushroom came ,start picking of mushroom . Do not take too much time ot pick 
","MADHYA PRADESH","HOSHANGABAD","KESLA","2019-01-21T09:22:14.31"

"NA","HORTICULTURE","Vegetables","Mushroom","	Plant Protection	","farmer want about mushroom production ?","Take wheat, soybean straw or rice straw {not older than 1 year], 
Soak it overnight in 50 liters of water + 3 grams bavistin +75 formalin   solution  then decant it before 2 hours of spanning.
Seprate the seed by crushing them. And fill uppermost and lowermost layer completely with span but in middile laye surface only pot in pripheral region followed by 2-2 inch straw layer . Make 2-3 holes in lower side and 10-15 holes in whole bag, and put it in a slanting surface to get out of remaining water .
After 15-20 days when whitish covering occurs hen hang it on bamboos and irrigate them every evening . Do not get them dried .
Check it out daily when mushroom came ,start picking of mushroom . Do not take too much time ot pick

IV- Flowering stage : 50-55 DAS
V- Grain filling stage : 70-75 DAS

"NA","AGRICULTURE","Cereals","Wheat","	Plant Protection	","Farmer needs information regarding WATER MANAGEMENT IN WHEAT CROP?
","Farmer needs information regarding WATER MANAGEMENT 
Recommended for the crop requires 4-6 irrigations depending on the soil type and rainfall.Wheat crop requires minimum of 5 irrigations at the following critical stages.
1.	Immediately after sowing
2.	Crown root initiation: 15-20 DAS 
3.	Active tillering stage: 35-40 DAS
4.	Flowering stage: 50-55 DAS
5.	Grain filling stage: 70-75 DAS
6.	Crown root initiation and flowering are the most critical stages. Water stagnation should be voided at the time of germination.","MADHYA PRADESH","UJJAIN","UJJAIN","2019-01-05T08:24:21.357"

"NA","HORTICULTURE","Condiments and Spices","Cumin","Field Preparation","Farmer needs information regarding about irrigation in cumin ?
","Immediately after the sowing of cumin should be given a light irrigation.
Keep in mind that during irrigation, the flow of water does not accelerate or else the seed flow will get busy due to rapid drift. By the end of one week of the sowing of irrigation, when the seed starts flowing.
If sprouting is not done after the second irrigation or the crust on the ground, then a light irrigation will be beneficial.
After this, the irrigation of 5 irrigations will be sufficient from 15 to 25 days according to the nature of the land and the weather.","MADHYA PRADESH","UJJAIN","KHACHAROD","2019-01-12T08:51:57.373"

"NA","AGRICULTURE","Others","Others","Bio-Pesticides and Bio-Fertilizers","Farmer Wants know information about  waste decomposer?","Dear farmer to use, add 200 liter water to 2 kg of jaggery and mix it well. Keep it for two days in summer and 4 days in winter. After this it is ready to use. Then mix one bucket solution with 200 liters of water in this hundred liters solution. Keep this solution in this way and keep adding this solution to the water while irrigating the fields. Drip irrigation can also be used with this solution. This will spread to the entire farm. Apart from this, once a month, the waste decomposer can be sprayed to remove the disease of crops.","MADHYA PRADESH","UJJAIN","BADNAGAR","2019-01-12T14:55:35.623"
"NA","AGRICULTURE","Others","Others","Organic Farming","farmer wants to know information about waste material compost ?
","How to prepare waste decomposer solution from the started culture?
Take 2 kg jaggery and mixed it in a plastic drum containing 200 liters water.
Now take 1 bottle of waste decomposer and pour all its contents in a plastic drum containing jaggery solution. Avoid direct contact of contents with hands.
Mix it properly with a wooden stick for uniform distribution of waste decomposer in a drum.
Cover the drum with a paper or cardboard and stir it every day once or twice.
After 5 days the solution of drum turns creamy.
Farmers could prepare the waste decomposer solution again and again from the above formed solution. For this, 20 liter of waste decomposer solution is added to a drum with 2 kg of jaggery and 20 liter water is added. Farmers can prepare continuously this solution from this waste decomposer for lifetime.","MADHYA PRADESH","UJJAIN","BADNAGAR","2019-01-12T14:57:37.463"

","The premium under the Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana is way less than the previous government or private crop insurance schemes. The premium amount for Kharif crops is 2 percent and 1.5 percent or the sum insured for Rabi crops. Karif and Rabi covers most food crops and oil crops cultivated in India. "NA","AGRICULTURE","Cereals","Wheat","	Water Management	","Farmer wants to know information about WATER MANAGEMENT in wheat? ","Recommended for The crop requires 4 - 6 irrigations depending on the soil type and rainfall. Wheat crop requires minimum of 5 irrigations at the following critical stages.
I – Immediately after sowing
II – Crown root initiation: 15-20 DAS 
III- Active tillering stage: 35-40 DAS
IV- Flowering stage: 50-55 DAS
V- Grain filling stage: 70-75 DAS
Crown root initiation and flowering are the most critical stages. Water stagnation should be voided at the time of germination.

"NA","AGRICULTURE","Cereals","Wheat","	Water Management	","Farmer wants to know information about WATER MANAGEMENT in wheat? ","Recommended for The crop requires 4 - 6 irrigations depending on the soil type and rainfall. Wheat crop requires minimum of 5 irrigations at the following critical stages.
I – Immediately after sowing
II – Crown root initiation: 15-20 DAS 
III- Active tillering stage: 35-40 DAS
IV- Flowering stage: 50-55 DAS
V- Grain filling stage: 70-75 DAS
Crown root initiation and flowering are the most critical stages. Water stagnation should be voided at the time of germination.
","MADHYA PRADESH","UJJAIN","UJJAIN","2019-01-15T09:07:05.103"

"NA","AGRICULTURE","Others","Others","Organic Farming","Farmer wants to know information regarding  vermicompost?
","Vermicompost
Method of preparation:
2 rows of bricks on top of the platform and the platform are added on top of the platform, are made up of huts for shade dry fodder, manure and 7-8 quintals kudhakrkt 3-4 quintals (garvej) hut shaped and baked spread manure jare, which gets 10-15 days, so that irrigation can be cooked at a temperature of compost. Thereafter 100 square feet per 10 thousand earthworms abandoned. After leaving worm stitches are covered with jute sacks, and 4 days to keep irrigation jare remain 45-50 percent humidity. Blocking shall be placed carefully over the wet air from the living microorganisms and earthworms to work or will not be able javegen dead.
Irrigation is stopped after 45 days and jute bags are removed. After removing the bags of compost moisture dries up and go down the earthworm. Then dried up vermi compost separate charge. 2 months in stitches, cast by the number of earthworms, are aware that the manure by hand, remove double pickaxe, spade or dib do not use. Tanken extracted from manure and dried in the shade, after filtering is stored in cover. Vermi compost in pots amount of 100 grams, one kilogram a year of crop plants require 6-8 quintals per acre. Wash using vermi platform would be nice to make two exhaust naliya wash the armadillo can be collected
","MADHYA PRADESH","UJJAIN","BADNAGAR","2019-01-15T15:03:20.493"

","With the introduction of the scheme, now farmers can apply for loan waiver by filling the form. From February 22, the amount will start reaching farmers' accounts. The benefit of the scheme will be to the farmers who have taken loan from the bank under the fertilizer-seed or KYC. Applications received from live portal farmers by online MP will be updated online. Farmers will be kept in three categories, green list, white list and pink list. The green list will be the names of the farmers who are linked to their base accounts. The white list will be the names of those farmers, whose accounts do not have a base link and they will be farmers in the pink list, whose names are incorrectly written in both these lists or the names are not there. The farmer who comes in the category will have to fill the form of that color, the farm farmer will get free. Gram Panchayat Bhavan and Ward Office will be listed on the list of borrower farmers

4.Flowering stage: 50-55 DAS
5.Grain filling stage: 70-75 DAS
6.Crown root initiation and flowering are the most critical stages. Water stagnation should be voided at the time of germination.

"NA","AGRICULTURE","Cereals","Wheat","	Water Management	","Farmer needs information regarding WATER MANAGEMENT in wheat? 
","Recommended for the crop requires 4-6 irrigations depending on the soil type and rainfall.Wheat crop requires minimum of 5 irrigations at the following critical stages.
1.	Immediately after sowing
2.	Crown root initiation: 15-20 DAS 
3.	Active tillering stage: 35-40 DAS
4.	Flowering stage: 50-55 DAS
5.	Grain filling stage: 70-75 DAS
6.	Crown root initiation and flowering are the most critical stages. Water stagnation should be voided at the time of germination.

"NA","AGRICULTURE","Cereals","Wheat","	Water Management	","farmer want to know information about WATER MANAGEMENT in wheat? 
","recommended for The crop requires 4 - 6 irrigations depending on the soil type and rainfall. Wheat crop requires minimum of 5 irrigations at the following critical stages.
I – Immediately after sowing
II – Crown root intiation : 15-20 DAS 
III- Active tillering stage : 35-40 DAS
IV- Flowering stage : 50-55 DAS
V- Grain filling stage : 70-75 DAS
Crown root initiation and flowering are the most critical stages. Water stagnation should be voided at the time of germination.

"NA","HORTICULTURE","Flowers","Marigold","Vegetative Propagation and Tissue Culture","Farmer wants to know about seed and spacing of  marigold ?","The seeds of marigold are  300-400 grams of seeds are required per acre, which is prepared in 500 sq. M. Seed bed, the seed depth in the seed bed is 1cm Should not exceed When the marigold is transmitted by cutting, it should be noted that the cutting should always be done with a new healthy plant, which is only 1-2 flowers, the size of the cutting should be 4 inches (10 cm) tall. Putting roux on this cutting should be applied in a sand-filled tray. After 20-22 days it should be planted in the field. Transplant: Mango flower Kharif, Rabi, Zayed are grown in the three seasons according to market demand. But the appropriate time to apply it is September-October. Different seasons are used at various distances, which is low
Kharif (June to July) - 60 x 45 cm
Rabi (September-October) - 45 x 45 cm
Zayed (February-March) - 45x30 cm","MADHYA PRADESH","UJJAIN","UJJAIN","2019-01-30T19:00:39.253"
